        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





A UAF occurs when dragging text into an iframe/embed element that is (re)loading.



<span class="line"><!---->A UAF occurs when dragging text into an iframe/embed element that is (re)loading.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This might be triggerable with other types of drag events, and with other types of embedded content.



<span class="line"><!---->This might be triggerable with other types of drag events, and with other types of embedded content.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Does NOT repro on asan-win32-release_x64-1069280 (last ASan build before commit identified below)



<span class="line"><!---->Does NOT repro on asan-win32-release_x64-1069280 (last ASan build before commit identified below)<!----></span>



<br>





DOES repro on asan-win32-release_x64-1069306 (first ASan build after commit identified below)



<span class="line"><!---->DOES repro on asan-win32-release_x64-1069306 (first ASan build after commit identified below)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Diff between both commits:



<span class="line"><!---->Diff between both commits:<!----></span>



<br>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+log/588f0d3bc4af1fb8ddf75fbdb68f44fedfc5d274..206f5caf5cefa269853c83d29879fe68517b37c9?pretty=fuller&n=10000



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+log/588f0d3bc4af1fb8ddf75fbdb68f44fedfc5d274..206f5caf5cefa269853c83d29879fe68517b37c9?pretty=fuller&amp;n=10000"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+log/588f0d3bc4af1fb8ddf75fbdb68f44fedfc5d274..206f5caf5cefa269853c83d29879fe68517b37c9?pretty=fuller&amp;n=10000<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Based on blame of ui\base\dragdrop\drop_target_event.cc line 28 (identified by ASan), and bisect above, commit 



<span class="line"><!---->Based on blame of ui\base\dragdrop\drop_target_event.cc line 28 (identified by ASan), and bisect above, commit <!----></span>





cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f"><!---->cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f<!----></a>





 is almost certainly causing the issue.



<span class="line"><!----> is almost certainly causing the issue.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





That commit seems to make changes that were meant to be safe *with* MiraclePtr/raw_ptr enabled, but I'm not aware of the timeline for this to be enabled, so it seems like a security issue right now. That commit is in Canary 109.0.5413.2 and Dev 109.0.5414.10 per 



<span class="line"><!---->That commit seems to make changes that were meant to be safe *with* MiraclePtr/raw_ptr enabled, but I'm not aware of the timeline for this to be enabled, so it seems like a security issue right now. That commit is in Canary 109.0.5413.2 and Dev 109.0.5414.10 per <!----></span>





https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/commit/cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/commit/cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f"><!---->https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/commit/cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





That commit (or other commits for 



<span class="line"><!---->That commit (or other commits for <!----></span>





issue 1357022



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1357022" title="Rewrite T&amp; member variable into raw_ref<T>"><!---->issue 1357022<!----></a>





) might have introduced UAFs in other areas. Again, not sure if that's intentional or not, but right now ASan says UAF, and AFAIK MiraclePtr isn't enabled in Canary/Dev where commit currently exists.



<span class="line"><!---->) might have introduced UAFs in other areas. Again, not sure if that's intentional or not, but right now ASan says UAF, and AFAIK MiraclePtr isn't enabled in Canary/Dev where commit currently exists.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: ASan build 1069306 (earliest repro build), build 1075493 (latest as of a couple of hours ago)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: ASan build 1069306 (earliest repro build), build 1075493 (latest as of a couple of hours ago)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 Version 21H2 (Build 19044.2251)



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 Version 21H2 (Build 19044.2251)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-iframe-uaf.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-iframe-uaf.html"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-iframe-uaf.html<!----></a>



<br>





2. Drag text over the (re)loading iframe/embed on the left



<span class="line"><!---->2. Drag text over the (re)loading iframe/embed on the left<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Observed: UAF while dragging over the iframe/embed



<span class="line"><!---->Observed: UAF while dragging over the iframe/embed<!----></span>

Discussing with other security team members there was some mixed opinions on whether this qualifies as "minimal user interaction". My personal opinion (as current security sheriff) is that, as this does not require interaction with browser features and is just web content, that this meets the "could a user be easily convinced to perform by a persuasive web page" test outlined in our severity guidelines [1] and thus should be considered minimal as a malicious page could easily convince a user to perform this drag action.



<span class="line"><!---->Discussing with other security team members there was some mixed opinions on whether this qualifies as "minimal user interaction". My personal opinion (as current security sheriff) is that, as this does not require interaction with browser features and is just web content, that this meets the "could a user be easily convinced to perform by a persuasive web page" test outlined in our severity guidelines [1] and thus should be considered minimal as a malicious page could easily convince a user to perform this drag action.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1]

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/master/docs/security/severity-guidelines.md#miracleptr-protection-against-use_after_free:~:text=could%20a%20user%20be%20easily%20convinced%20to%20perform%20by%20a%20persuasive%20web%20page"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/master/docs/security/severity-guidelines.md#miracleptr-protection-against-use_after_free:~:text=could%20a%20user%20be%20easily%20convinced%20to%20perform%20by%20a%20persuasive%20web%20page<!----></a>

Based on this comment of another Drag-and-Drop UAF bug, this *might* be triggerable with a compromised renderer without user interaction: 



<span class="line"><!---->Based on this comment of another Drag-and-Drop UAF bug, this *might* be triggerable with a compromised renderer without user interaction: <!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1153595#c4



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1153595#c4"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1153595#c4<!----></a>

I'll need to verify that later this week, though. Either way, it's very easy to trigger with regular renderer, and PoC probably can be improved to further increase reliability (might work to improve PoC within a week or two if it'll help).

While looking at how this code works, saw this CL [1] from 2019 which added most of the code path in the stack trace. One of the CL comments mentions this PoC [2] was hitting a DCHECK when dragging an image between two iframes. Using that exact PoC, I was also able to quickly repro this UAF by dragging an image between both cross-site iframes. Not sure if that old DCHECK is related to the current behavior, but did help me find another way to repro.



<span class="line"><!---->While looking at how this code works, saw this CL [1] from 2019 which added most of the code path in the stack trace. One of the CL comments mentions this PoC [2] was hitting a DCHECK when dragging an image between two iframes. Using that exact PoC, I was also able to quickly repro this UAF by dragging an image between both cross-site iframes. Not sure if that old DCHECK is related to the current behavior, but did help me find another way to repro.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Based on [2], I've created a simplified PoC [3] which triggers UAF immediately after starting drag.



<span class="line"><!---->Based on [2], I've created a simplified PoC [3] which triggers UAF immediately after starting drag.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Worth noting that some simple variations led to no repro, so it does seem like the renderer has some influence over the UAF trigger.



<span class="line"><!---->Worth noting that some simple variations led to no repro, so it does seem like the renderer has some influence over the UAF trigger.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Most notably, at least one of the iframes has to be cross-site (OOPIF), and both iframes have to overlap with each other by at least 1px. There may be other ways of triggering this, but this seemed like the most reliable.



<span class="line"><!---->Most notably, at least one of the iframes has to be cross-site (OOPIF), and both iframes have to overlap with each other by at least 1px. There may be other ways of triggering this, but this seemed like the most reliable.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->2. Start to drag image.<!----></span>

Observed: UAF immediately when starting drag.



<span class="line"><!---->Observed: UAF immediately when starting drag.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This also works when dragging links (like in original report's PoC) and images within HTML pages (like in [2]), so the attacker can get creative with how to convince the user to drag. I imagine the JS APIs related to dragging might also help an attacker.



<span class="line"><!---->This also works when dragging links (like in original report's PoC) and images within HTML pages (like in [2]), so the attacker can get creative with how to convince the user to drag. Using the test case [1] added in that same CL, I was also able to repro. The test case specifically tests top-level page content overlapping the iframe. This only requires one cross-site iframe + an element from the top-level page overlapping any portion of the iframe.

Attached PoC for single click with compromised renderer.



<span class="line"><!---->Attached PoC for single click with compromised renderer.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Setup compromised renderer: 



<span class="line"><!---->Setup compromised renderer: <!----></span>



<br>





1. Checkout Chromium commit 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Checkout Chromium commit <!----></span>





a4537e1eb7038c62232f88c9807a13139612efce



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/a4537e1eb7038c62232f88c9807a13139612efce"><!---->a4537e1eb7038c62232f88c9807a13139612efce<!----></a>





 (should also work with HEAD or any recent revision after commit 



<span class="line"><!----> (should also work with HEAD or any recent revision after commit <!----></span>





cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f"><!---->cf5c86ba22fcf6752ba8c5af6cde8bbc04e8e67f<!----></a>





 on Nov 9th)



<span class="line"><!----> on Nov 9th)<!----></span>



<br>





2. Apply attached renderer patch: `git apply renderer.patch`



<span class="line"><!---->2. Apply attached renderer patch: `git apply renderer.patch`<!----></span>



<br>





3. Build Chromium ASan (is_asan=true in args.gn)



<span class="line"><!---->3. Build Chromium ASan (is_asan=true in args.gn)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Run PoC using build above:



<span class="line"><!---->Run PoC using build above:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-oopif-uaf-single-click.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-oopif-uaf-single-click.html"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/drag-oopif-uaf-single-click.html<!----></a>



<br>





2. Click anywhere in box (essentially anywhere in the page).



<span class="line"><!---->2. Click anywhere in box (essentially anywhere in the page).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Observed: UAF immediately on mouse down.



<span class="line"><!---->Observed: UAF immediately on mouse down.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If it does not repro the first time, move mouse (even slightly, like in earlier PoCs) and then click again.



<span class="line"><!---->If it does not repro the first time, move mouse (even slightly, like in earlier PoCs) and then click again.<!----></span>



<br>





You may need to adjust the trigger() interval delay if you hit STATUS_BREAKPOINT in renderer process (increase delay) or if it's not 99% reliable for you (decrease delay).



<span class="line"><!---->You may need to adjust the trigger() interval delay if you hit STATUS_BREAKPOINT in renderer process (increase delay) or if it's not 99% reliable for you (decrease delay).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In a normal renderer, a user drag is initiated when a user holds down their primary mouse button and then moves the mouse a few pixels without releasing the mouse button (see earlier PoCs).



<span class="line"><!---->In a normal renderer, a user drag is initiated when a user holds down their primary mouse button and then moves the mouse a few pixels without releasing the mouse button (see earlier PoCs).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A compromised renderer can reduce friction by calling StartDragging() [1,2] to initiate the drag without the user having to hold+move mouse. Because the drag will be cancelled shortly after if the mouse is not pressed, the renderer repeatedly calls StartDragging() (on a 300ms delay in PoC) to try to stay in the dragging state. Once a drag is in progress, a click is sufficient to trigger the UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->A compromised renderer can reduce friction by calling StartDragging() [1,2] to initiate the drag without the user having to hold+move mouse. Because the drag will be cancelled shortly after if the mouse is not pressed, the renderer repeatedly calls StartDragging() (on a 300ms delay in PoC) to try to stay in the dragging state. Once a drag is in progress, a click is sufficient to trigger the UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I think the PoC works because the browser calls DragDropController::DragUpdate() [3] when the mouse is dragged (ui::ET_MOUSE_DRAGGED) [4]. I think a click while drag is in progress (even if initiated by renderer) will emit ui::ET_MOUSE_DRAGGED, therefore it reaches that path. Since the UAF repros immediately on mouse down (as opposed to mouse up), I don't think this PoC is reaching the ui::ET_MOUSE_RELEASED/Drop() [5] path. This code path analysis is speculative based on observed behavior, but will try to confirm soon.



<span class="line"><!---->I think the PoC works because the browser calls DragDropController::DragUpdate() [3] when the mouse is dragged (ui::ET_MOUSE_DRAGGED) [4]. I think a click while drag is in progress (even if initiated by renderer) will emit ui::ET_MOUSE_DRAGGED, therefore it reaches that path. Since the UAF repros immediately on mouse down (as opposed to mouse up), I don't think this PoC is reaching the ui::ET_MOUSE_RELEASED/Drop() [5] path. This code path analysis is speculative based on observed behavior, but will try to confirm soon.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>



<br>





Based on my current understanding, there's a chance of this being reproducible without user interaction with compromised renderer, but haven't quite gotten there yet.



<span class="line"><!---->Based on my current understanding, there's a chance of this being reproducible without user interaction with compromised renderer, but haven't quite gotten there yet.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Possibly related: the PoC sometimes also triggers a null read on click if the page has not fully loaded/rendered yet (hence the PoC waiting for the window load event). This is less reliable but does occur; you can test it using by modifying the PoC to start calling trigger() immediately. Since my ASan build currently isn't symbolized, not sure what's causing the null read but presumably it's related to the code causing the UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->Possibly related: the PoC sometimes also triggers a null read on click if the page has not fully loaded/rendered yet (hence the PoC waiting for the window load event). Since my ASan build currently isn't symbolized, not sure what's causing the null read but presumably it's related to the code causing the UAF.<!----></span>

Running ASan build 1076443 or my custom ASan build with --enable-features=PartitionAllocBackupRefPtr:asan-enable-dereference-check/false/asan-enable-instantiation-check/false [1] does not seem to result in an ASan-detectable UAF using any of the PoCs provided. With either of those checks enabled, we hit the deref check (original report) or the instantiation check, both at the same spot (drop_target_event.cc:28). There might be other code paths that do result in a UAF with deref check disabled, but haven't had a chance to explore those (and probably won't given this appears to be a duplicate of other issue).



<span class="line"><!---->Running ASan build 1076443 or my custom ASan build with --enable-features=PartitionAllocBackupRefPtr:asan-enable-dereference-check/false/asan-enable-instantiation-check/false [1] does not seem to result in an ASan-detectable UAF using any of the PoCs provided. With either of those checks enabled, we hit the deref check (original report) or the instantiation check, both at the same spot (drop_target_event.cc:28). There might be other code paths that do result in a UAF with deref check disabled, but haven't had a chance to explore those (and probably won't given this appears to be a duplicate of other issue).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;

        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;

          white-space: nowrap;

          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);

          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
